Observed on Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa-Navam─л tithi of Vai┼Ы─Бkhaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 3047 (kali era).
A native of Chera country, son of S┼лryan─Бr─Бyaс╣Зamakhi, by name Chinnaya, having secured excellence in S─Бhitya by the infinite or immeasurable or unbound grace of goddess Gaur─л, who was pleased with worship, the sage by name ─Аn─Бndaj├▒─Бna prefixed with the term тАШBhagavatтАЩ the author of a collection of expository texts on the works of ─Аc─Бrya, lived in the K─Бmakoс╣нi P─лс╣нha of the ─Аc─Бrya, the author of a commentary on Brahmas┼лtras. This accomplished knower of Brahman having got rid of the ignorance by the immaculate splendour of the moon-like ┼Ъuddh─Бnandamun─лndra, spreading the path of non-dualism protecting the world/earth for sixty-nine years, then approaching ┼Ъr─л┼Ыail─Б, on the way, attained blissful liberation on the ninth day of the dark fortnight in the month of R─Бdh─Б (Vai┼Ы─Бkha) of the year Krodhana.

Observed on Kс╣Ыс╣гс╣Зa-Caturda┼Ы─л tithi of Vai┼Ы─Бkhaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 2738 (kali era).
This Sarvaj├▒─Бtman, who was born to Vardhana got initiated into asceticism even before the age of seven by ┼Ъri ┼Ъaс╣Еkara himself on being delighted to have had debate with him on the banks of river T─Бmraparс╣Зi; he spent seventy years along with Sure┼Ыvara in that P─лс╣нha and then lived in that Maс╣нha for forty two years. The sage known as Sarvaj├▒a attained union with his own Self by doing service at the lotus feet of ┼Ъri Padmap─Бda, who was dear to the ─Аc─Бrya (┼Ъri ┼Ъaс╣Еkara) and imparting the unparallel doctrine through Cinmudr─Б to the saint by name Brahmasvar┼лpa who served with love and faith at the feet of the master who was holding the pontiff-dom of the Dv─Бravat─л maс╣нha. The sage Sarvaj├▒─Бtman whose works such as Saс╣Бkс╣гepa┼Ы─Бr─лraka showed clearly/elaborately the collective meaning of the words hidden in the great commentatorial works on Advaita merged in the Supreme on the fourteenth day of the dark fortnight in the month of Vai┼Ы─Бkha in the Nala year of the Kali era 2737 at K─Б├▒ci ┼Ъri ┼Ъaс╣Еkara Maс╣нha.

рд╢реНрд░реАрдирд┐рд╡рд╛рд╕рдордЩреНрдЧрд╛рдкреБрд░реЗ рд╕рд╛рдХреНрд╖рд╛рддреНрдХрд╛рд░-рд╡реИрднрд╡реЛрддреНрд╕рд╡рдГ

Observed on ┼Ъukla-с╣вaс╣гс╣нh─л tithi of Jyaiс╣гс╣нhaс╕е (lunar) month (S┼лryodayaс╕е/puurvaviddha). According to historical evidences, dated 22nd March 1540 CE, the Temple was brought to worship by doing Jeernoddhaarana by Chinni Thirumalacharyulu, the grandson of great saint Sri Talapaka Annamacharyulu. In 1940 CE. an Archaka Swamulu by name Sundararaju from Tamilnadu came to Srinivasa Mangapuram. He shared his dream with villagers by saying that in his dream Lord Venkateswara Swamy appeared and asked him to bring the temple to Past Vaibhavam (glorious) by performing Deepa Naivedya Aaradhana and Lord disppeared. As per the Lord words, Archaka Swami Sundaraju performed first pooja on July 1940 which was coincided on Ashada Shudda Shasti Day with the help of village elders. To mark the auspicious day of revival of Nitya Pooja Kainkaryam, TTD has been conducting this festival as Sakshatkara Vaibhavotsavam on Ashada Shuddha Shasti Day in the Jyaishta month every year.

He, Saccitsukha, having instituted Citsukha in his place, attained siddhi on the seventh day of the bright fortnight of the month of Vс╣Ыс╣гabha in the year Khara.

Then having spent thirty-eight years in the P─лс╣нha of the Universal Preceptor, He merged in Brahman, the eternal free from joy and sorrow and the everlasting on the eighth day of the bright fortnight in Vс╣Ыс╣гa month of the year Akс╣гaya in the Kali era 3468 in the place called Kal─Бpur in Kashmir.

рдХрд╛рдЮреНрдЪреА ремрез рдЬрдЧрджреНрдЧреБрд░реБ рд╢реНрд░реА-рдорд╣рд╛рджреЗрд╡реЗрдиреНрджреНрд░ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рддреА рек рдЖрд░рд╛рдзрдирд╛ #реиренрел

Observed on ┼Ъukla-Navam─л tithi of Jyaiс╣гс╣нhaс╕е (lunar) month (Apar─Бhс╣Зaс╕е/vyaapti). The event has been commemorated since it occurred in 4847 (kali era).
Here (in this world) the best among preceptors by name Mah─Бdevendra adorned the incomparable seat of preceptor for forty-two years; thus the great Yogi realised the Self and attained siddhi on the ninth day of bright fortnight in the month of Jyeс╣гс╣нha in the year Krodhana. ─Аtmabodha, who wrote a commentary Suс╣гam─Б on ┼Ъr─л Sad─Б┼ЫivabrahmendraтАЩs Gururatnam─Бlika also belonged to this period (a contemporary of this preceptor). Only during this period, the Jagadguru Maс╣нha moved out of K─Б├▒ci. The place where this present preceptor attained siddhi was the wellknown Tiruvottiyur situated in the north of Madras (┼Ъalivahana era 1664).
